Blackrock Foundry Opens this Week
Only Normal and Heroic Blackrock Foundry will be open this week. LFR's first wing opens in two weeks and last wing opens in seven weeks.
It won’t be long before you’ll be able to take the assault against the Iron Horde to the next level in new Raid content. To help you plan your attack, we’ve broken down the unlock schedule for Blackrock Foundry and the third Draenor world boss – Rukhmar. Will you be ready?
Those who plan to jump into the action in the Raid Finder will need a minimum item level of 635. Here's the rundown:

February 3, 2015:

Blackrock Foundry opens with Normal and Heroic difficulties available.
World boss Rukhmar becomes available in Spires of Arak.


February 10, 2015:

Mythic difficulty becomes available.


February 17, 2015:

Raid Finder Wing 1: Slagworks (Gruul, Oregorger, and The Blast Furnace) unlocks.


February 24, 2015:

Raid Finder Wing 2: The Black Forge (Hans’gar and Franzok, Flamebender Ka’graz, and Kromog ) unlocks.


March 10, 2015:

Raid Finder Wing 3: Iron Assembly (Beastlord Darmac, Operator Thogar, and The Iron Maidens) unlocks.


March 24, 2015:

Raid Finder Wing 4: Blackhand’s Crucible (Blackhand) unlocks.



AskMrRobot - Combat Infographics
AskMrRobot is launching a new feature just in time for Blackrock Foundry, with BRF boss infographics (http://blog.askmrrobot.com/2015/02/blackrock-foundry-infographics/) starting Wednesday morning. Combat Infographics (http://blog.askmrrobot.com/2015/01/combat-infographics/) give you an at a glance idea of how well you and your raid are doing at things like avoiding damage, dealing damage, healing, killing adds, and more.


http://media.mmo-champion.com/images/news/2015/february/AMRCombatInfographic.jpg (http://blog.askmrrobot.com/2015/01/combat-infographics/)


Icy Veins - Blackrock Foundry Guides
Our friends over at Icy Veins are finishing up their Blackrock Foundry guides (http://www.icy-veins.com/wow/blackrock-foundry-raid), so be sure to take a look so that you are ready to go this week.

Legendary Ring Quest
The opening of Blackrock Foundry should allow you to complete Chapter III: The Foundry Falls (http://ptr.wowdb.com/achievements/9642-chapter-iii-the-foundry-falls) by completing specific parts of Blackrock Foundry and collecting 900 x Elemental Rune (http://ptr.wowdb.com/items/115510-elemental-rune). The Blackhand's Secret quest in the achievement still hasn't activated on live or PTR realms, so we don't know exactly what it requires or rewards yet.
